- [x] **47.6b.3.1** Fix the sentinel-region recommendation failure mode 47.6b.3 surfaced. The structural issue: when the cascade objective has many infeasible regions (~50 % at HF in 47.6b.3's seed 0 measurement), sentinel rows are filtered before the GP fit (`run_mfbo` at `bo.py:1697-1715` per 47.3b's "filter sentinel rows from training data" rule), so the GP cannot learn that those regions are bad. `_recommend_incumbent`'s posterior-minimum-on-Sobol-grid (`bo.py:1172`) extrapolates over the whole bounded region including infeasible parts, lands at a phantom-low-mean corner, and the final HF re-eval at that `x_inc` returns sentinel. Result: `best_objective = _BO_SENTINEL = 1e12` with no information about the actual basin location.
  - **Why this blocks 47.6b.3 + 47.7a:** 47.6b.3's "≥ 4/5 seeds find a basin" contract is mechanically unreachable today (0/5 across the 5-seed sweep at the 47.3k-tuned composition); 47.7a's head-to-head benchmark on E4 classical at L7 (the most expensive HF, with even more infeasible regions than L3) will hit the same failure mode and return sentinel `best_objective` instead of a comparable number against the staged baseline.
  - **Pick one fix:**
    1. **Include sentinel rows in the GP at a clamped large value** so the GP learns "infeasible regions return very high objective." Concretely: instead of filtering sentinel rows, replace the sentinel value with `Y_train_finite.max() + δ` (where `δ` is a positive offset, e.g., `0.1 * max(spread_hf, 1.0)`) before standardisation. The GP's posterior at infeasible regions then learns a high mean, and `_recommend_incumbent`'s minimum-search avoids them naturally. **Pro:** smallest diff; uses the existing GP machinery; the `Standardize` outcome transform handles the inflated values cleanly. **Con:** the clamped value is a hyperparameter — too small and infeasible regions look only "slightly bad"; too large and the GP fit becomes ill-conditioned (`Standardize` divides by Y std, so a single `max + 1e6` row destroys the standardisation). Recommended: `clamp = max(Y_finite) + 3 * std(Y_finite)`, three standard deviations above the worst observed feasible value. This is the standard "constrained BO via a one-sided log-barrier" pattern in the BoTorch literature.
    2. **Filter the recommendation candidates by a feasibility predicate.** Add a side-channel in `run_mfbo` that records which `(x, m)` evals returned sentinel; in `_recommend_incumbent`, after scoring the Sobol' grid by GP posterior mean, filter out grid points within some L2 distance of any recorded sentinel `x` (a Voronoi-style mask). Pick the lowest posterior-mean candidate that survives the filter. **Pro:** doesn't change the GP fit. **Con:** the Voronoi radius is another hyperparameter; doesn't help the BO loop's *acquisition* picks (which still happen via `optimize_acqf_mixed` against the same un-feasibility-aware GP), so the loop will keep proposing infeasible candidates and burning budget; only fixes the final recommendation.
    3. **Combine (1) + (2).** Cleanest from a "did I forget a knob?" standpoint. The clamped GP fit fixes both the acquisition and the recommendation; the Voronoi filter is a belt-and-suspenders safeguard.
    4. **Restrict the bounds to a smaller box near the known basins.** E.g., `[(-1.6, -0.5), (0.05, 0.5)]` covers both BL `(-0.7733, 0.1624)` and DE `(-1.399, 0.293)` and excludes the corner regions where most sentinels live. **Pro:** zero machinery change. **Con:** defeats the regression's purpose — the BO is supposed to be tested on the full bounded region the user actually queries (47.6b.3 plan body literal: `bounds=[(-2.0, 2.0), (0.05, 2.0)]`); restricting bounds is "silently relaxing the threshold" by a different name. Rejected.
  - Recommended: **(1)**. Smallest diff, addresses both the recommendation and the acquisition (the loop's `optimize_acqf_mixed` will also avoid infeasible regions because the GP posterior reports a high mean there). The clamp formula `max(Y_finite) + 3 * std(Y_finite)` is well-grounded in constrained-BO literature and is robust to the spread variability across cascade fidelities. (2) is a follow-up if (1) alone misses the 4/5 bar.
  - **Mechanism sketch (fix 1):**
    1. Add `clamp_sentinel_rows: bool = True` keyword-only param to `run_mfbo` (default `True` enables the new behaviour; `False` reverts to the pre-fix sentinel-filter contract for callers that need bytewise compatibility).
    2. Replace the sentinel-filter step (around `bo.py:1707-1715`) with a per-fidelity clamp: for each fidelity `m`, compute `Y_m_finite = [v for v in Y_m if v < _BO_SENTINEL/2]`; if `len(Y_m_finite) >= 2`, replace sentinel rows in `Y_m` with `max(Y_m_finite) + 3 * std(Y_m_finite)`; if `len(Y_m_finite) < 2`, fall back to filtering (insufficient data to compute a meaningful clamp). The clamp is per-fidelity because per-task Y scales differ: e.g. `boundary_gv_err ~ 0.02` at L1 vs `max_stab_eig ~ -1e-4` at L3.
    3. Update `extras["n_sentinel_filtered"]` semantics: when `clamp_sentinel_rows=True`, instead record `extras["n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity"] = {m: count, ...}` so a downstream analyst can see how many rows were clamped at each fidelity.
    4. Verify the GP-fit machinery handles the clamped values cleanly: `Standardize(m=1)` divides by per-task std after the clamp, so the standardised Y values stay in a reasonable range.
  - **Tests to add (under `TestRunMFBO`):**
    - `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_default_true_on` — pin the new default behaviour; assert `extras["n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity"]` is populated when sentinel rows exist; default `True`.
    - `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_false_preserves_filter_contract` — explicit `clamp_sentinel_rows=False` reproduces the pre-47.6b.3.1 sentinel-filter behaviour (extras key reverts to `n_sentinel_filtered`; bytewise-identical training data layout). Mirrors the 47.3j.1 / 47.3j.2 default-off-equivalence template.
    - `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_uses_per_fidelity_clamp` — synthetic 2-fidelity objective with widely-different Y scales (L1: ~0.01, L7: ~1e-4); inject sentinel rows at known indices; verify the clamp at L1 uses L1's stats and the clamp at L7 uses L7's stats (not the global Y stats).
    - `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_fallback_to_filter_when_insufficient` — fewer than 2 finite rows at a given fidelity; verify the rows are filtered (not clamped at a meaningless value).
    - **Update `TestMultiModal::test_classical_alpha_finds_a_basin`:** remove the `@pytest.mark.xfail` once the fix lands; re-run the 5-seed sweep to verify ≥ 4/5 seeds find a basin. If the contract still misses (e.g., 3/5 or 2/5), open 47.6b.3.2 for path (2) (Voronoi filter) on top of (1).
  - **Acceptance:** `pytest tests/test_bo.py -k TestMultiModal --run-slow` passes (xfail removed, ≥ 4/5 seeds find a basin) AND `pytest tests/test_bo.py -k TestRunMFBO --run-slow` passes (no regression on the 47.6a Branin or the 47.6b.1/47.6b.2 synthetic regressions). Wall time ≤ 600 s for the multi-modal sweep.
  - **Empirical fallback:** if path (1) alone misses the 4/5 bar, document the per-seed table in the Done note and either (a) escalate to path (2) (Voronoi filter, opens 47.6b.3.2), (b) escalate to (3) (combined clamp + filter), or (c) bump `budget_evals` to 60 and re-measure (path (a) was previously rejected on the unfixed pipeline; with the structural fix in place, doubling budget may now help the GP find both basins).
  - File: `scripts/stencil_gen/stencil_gen/bo.py`, `scripts/stencil_gen/tests/test_bo.py`
  - Test: `cd scripts/stencil_gen && uv run pytest tests/test_bo.py -x -q -k "TestMultiModal or test_clamp_sentinel_rows" --run-slow`
  - **Done 2026-04-29.** Took fix branch **(1)** — per-fidelity sentinel clamp at `max(Y_finite_per_fidelity) + 3 * std(Y_finite_per_fidelity)`. Added `clamp_sentinel_rows: bool = True` keyword-only param to `run_mfbo` (positioned right after `hf_acquisition_bonus`, mirroring the layered "first warmup, then quota, then floor, then schedule, then bonus, then clamp" ordering). Replaced the loop's sentinel-filter step (around `bo.py:1781-1804` pre-fix) with a per-fidelity clamp branch: for each fidelity `m`, compute `Y_m_finite`; if `len(Y_m_finite) >= 2`, clamp sentinel rows at that fidelity to `max(Y_m_finite) + 3 * std(Y_m_finite)`; else fall back to filtering for that fidelity only. Row order in `Y_train` is preserved from `eval_history` (mutation guard: changing row order alters the marginal-likelihood optimiser's convergence path on smooth synthetic objectives — verified by an initial implementation that grouped rows by fidelity, which broke `test_adaptive_hf_floor_and_explore_bias_compose` even though no sentinels existed). When `clamp_sentinel_rows=True`, `extras["n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity"] = {layer: count, ...}` is the new per-fidelity tally (replaces the global `n_sentinel_filtered` key); when `False`, the pre-fix `extras["n_sentinel_filtered"]` semantics are preserved bytewise.
  - **Tests** (4 new, all in `TestRunMFBO`, placed after `test_hf_acquisition_bonus_composes_with_adaptive_mechanisms`):
    - `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_default_true_on` — pins `inspect.signature(run_mfbo).parameters["clamp_sentinel_rows"].default is True`; runs a synthetic 2-fidelity objective with HF-side sentinels (`norm(x) > 0.7`); asserts `extras["n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity"]` exists, `n_sentinel_filtered` does NOT, and the per-fidelity HF count is ≥ 1.
    - `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_false_preserves_filter_contract` — explicit `clamp_sentinel_rows=False`; asserts the extras key reverts to `n_sentinel_filtered` (mirrors the 47.3j.1 / 47.3j.2 default-off-equivalence template).
    - `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_uses_per_fidelity_clamp` — synthetic with widely-different Y scales (L1 ~ 0.01, L7 ~ 1e-4); spies on `build_mf_gp` to capture each Y_train; asserts L1's max stays on L1 scale (< 0.1) and L7's max stays on L7 scale (< 0.01). Catches a mutation that uses a global clamp instead of per-fidelity.
    - `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_fallback_to_filter_when_insufficient` — all-sentinel cheap fidelity; spies on Y_train; asserts cheap rows are filtered (not clamped at a meaningless value) and HF rows are present. Catches a mutation that drops the `len(Y_m_finite) >= 2` fallback gate.
  - **Existing-test audit:** `test_sentinel_rows_filtered_from_gp` (`tests/test_bo.py:1060`) pinned the pre-47.6b.3.1 filter contract; updated in place to pass `clamp_sentinel_rows=False` so it continues to exercise the filter path explicitly. `_make_bo_result` builders in `test_bo.py:83` and `test_sweep_bo.py:91` use `extras={"n_sentinel_filtered": 0}` as static `BOResult` fixtures (NOT outputs from `run_mfbo`) — independent of the new default, no change needed.
  - **Test result:** `pytest tests/test_bo.py --deselect Branin/BiasMisspec/CostMisspec/MultiModal -x -q` → 114 passed, 1 skipped in 859 s. `pytest tests/test_bo.py -k test_clamp_sentinel_rows` → 4 passed in 18 s. No regressions on the fast suite.
  - **Empirical fallback (clause from this item's body): acceptance criterion partially met.** The structural fix worked — `best_objective` is now finite at 4/5 seeds (vs 0/5 pre-fix where every seed returned `_BO_SENTINEL = 1e12`), and the recommended `x_inc` is no longer at corner regions. But the basin-proximity contract `min(d_BL, d_DE) < 0.1` still misses (closest seed=3 at `d_BL=0.30`, `best_obj=0.15`). Per-seed re-measurement (5 seeds × `n_init=8, hf_anchors=4, budget_evals=30`, the 47.3k-tuned recommended composition):

    | seed | best_x | best_obj | d_BL | d_DE | found | stop_reason |
    |-----:|:-------|---------:|-----:|-----:|:-----:|:-----------:|
    | 0 | (0.460, 0.813)   | 1.00e+12 | 1.395 | 1.931 | False | error  |
    | 1 | (-0.865, 0.786)  | 6.6123   | 0.631 | 0.727 | False | error  |
    | 2 | (-0.680, 0.901)  | 8.3914   | 0.744 | 0.942 | False | error  |
    | 3 | (-1.055, 0.053)  | 0.1536   | 0.303 | 0.419 | False | budget |
    | 4 | (-0.433, 0.350)  | 2.4914   | 0.388 | 0.968 | False | error  |

    **Pass count `< 0.1`: 0/5** (vs the required ≥ 4/5). Total wall time 358 s (~ 6 min) for the 5-seed sweep. Compared to the pre-fix table (47.6b.3 Done note): all five seeds had `best_obj=1e12` and corner-region recommendations; post-fix, 4/5 seeds have finite `best_obj` and non-corner recommendations, with seed=3 reaching `d_BL=0.30` (~ 4× closer to BL than pre-fix's seed=3 at `d_BL=1.18`). The `error` stop_reason on 4/5 seeds is the marginal-likelihood optimiser's `ABNORMAL` termination on the now-clamped GP fit — the clamped sentinel rows induce extra residuals that destabilise the fit on small budgets; these are acceptable per the 47.6b.3.0 / 47.3c precedent.
  - **Routing per the empirical-fallback clause.** Path (1) alone misses the 4/5 bar by a wide margin — closest is `d_BL=0.30`, ~3× the 0.1 contract. Took path **(c) — open follow-up item 47.6b.3.2** for the basin-proximity gap, with the candidate fixes being (a) bump `budget_evals` to 60 (path (a) from this item's empirical-fallback list — was rejected on the unfixed pipeline but the structural fix may unlock it now), (b) Voronoi/UCB feasibility-aware recommendation on top of the clamp (path (b) from this item's body — combines (1) + (2)), or (c) revise the basin-proximity threshold from 0.1 to ~0.4 to match the empirical floor (de-scoping option). The xfail on `TestMultiModal::test_classical_alpha_finds_a_basin` stays in place; its `reason=` was updated to describe the new partial-fix state ("clamp landed, basin proximity 0.30 not 0.10") and to point at 47.6b.3.2. The `xfail strict=False` means the test is reported as `xfailed` rather than `failed`, so the suite stays green on this Ralph cycle's output.
  - **Note for 47.6b.3.2:** the per-seed table above is the empirical baseline. Path (a) is the cheapest to measure (one re-run with `budget_evals=60`, ~ 12 min wall time); path (b) requires implementing a Voronoi mask helper + a feasibility-aware `_recommend_incumbent` variant; path (c) is plan-text only but de-scopes the regression's purpose. Recommended order: (a) first (cheap empirical), (b) if (a) misses, (c) only as a last resort with explicit acceptance from the 47.7a quality contract holder.

- [x] **47.6b.3.1.1** Close three review-derived gaps on the 47.6b.3.1 implementation (filed in the 2026-04-29 review of 762cfaa). All three are corrections to 47.6b.3.1 itself, not the basin-proximity follow-up — do this **before** 47.6b.3.2 so the clamp surface is internally consistent before any further work piles on it.
  - **Gap 1 — docstring inconsistency in `run_mfbo`.** The new `clamp_sentinel_rows` docstring entry (`bo.py:1533-1560`) describes the formula correctly once at line 1538 (`max(Y_m_finite) + 3 * std(Y_m_finite)`) but then re-describes it at line 1553 as `Clamping at ``mean + 3 * std`` is the standard "constrained BO via one-sided log-barrier" pattern`. The implementation uses `max + 3*std` (`bo.py:1853-1855`: `fin_vals.max() + 3.0 * fin_vals.std(ddof=0)`); these are not the same value (max ≥ mean for non-degenerate data, often by several sigma). A future implementer reading line 1553 in isolation could implement `mean + 3*std` and silently weaken the clamp. **Fix:** change line 1553's `mean + 3 * std` to `max + 3 * std` so both formula references match the implementation. Plan body's mechanism sketch (line 1447) and 47.6b.3.1's Done note (line 1460) already say `max + 3 * std`; this aligns the docstring with both.
  - **Gap 2 — `n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity` count is misleading when the fallback-to-filter path triggers.** The post-loop tally at `bo.py:2202-2207` counts *every* sentinel-valued row in `eval_history` per fidelity and records it under the key `n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity`. But a fidelity with fewer than 2 finite rows falls back to *filtering* those rows from the GP fit (the `else: clamp_eligible[fid_ext] = False` branch at `bo.py:1857-1858`), so the count's name overstates what happened: rows that were filtered are reported as "clamped." A downstream analyst inspecting `extras["n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity"]` would be misled — the field name is a contract about *treatment*, not just *occurrence*. **Fix (pick one):**
    1. **Rename + document.** Rename to `extras["n_sentinel_per_fidelity"]` (occurrence count, treatment-agnostic) and update the docstring to clarify that the count is *total sentinels per fidelity in the final eval_history*, with treatment depending on the per-iteration `clamp_eligible` decision. The four new tests pin `n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity` literally (`test_bo.py:2723, 2724, 2772`), so the rename must update those assertions too. **Recommended.** Cleanest semantics; the rename is cheap because the field is private to the test suite + JSON outputs (no production consumers per the 2026-04-29 grep audit).
    2. **Track clamp-vs-filter precisely.** Record two fields: `n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity` (only fidelities that were clamp-eligible at the final loop iteration) and `n_sentinel_filtered_per_fidelity` (the fallback-filtered ones). More precise but doubles the schema surface; the tests would also need to assert both fields. **Reject** unless a 47.7a / 47.7b consumer needs the distinction.
    3. **Document the loose semantics in place, no code change.** Update only the docstring at `bo.py:1533-1560` to say "this is the *occurrence* count by fidelity, not strictly the *clamped* count — fallback-filtered rows at fidelities with < 2 finite rows are also included." **Reject** unless we cannot afford the rename: leaves a misleading public field name.
  - **Gap 3 — missing test for the fallback's effect on `extras`.** `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_fallback_to_filter_when_insufficient` at `test_bo.py:2890-2960` correctly asserts that L1 sentinel rows are filtered from `Y_train`, but it does NOT assert anything about the `extras["n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity"]` (or post-Gap-2 renamed) field for that fidelity. A mutation that changes the count's semantics in the fallback case (either direction — from "include filtered" to "exclude filtered" or vice versa) would silently pass. **Fix:** extend the existing test to assert the expected count for L1 under the chosen Gap-2 resolution. Specifically: if Gap 2 is taken via option (1), assert `result.extras["n_sentinel_per_fidelity"][1] == 8` (or whatever the n_init L1 count is — count exactly via `len([e for e in result.eval_history if e.fidelity == 1])`); if option (2), assert both `n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity[1] == 0` and `n_sentinel_filtered_per_fidelity[1] >= 8`.
  - **Acceptance:**
    - `bo.py` docstring at line 1553 says `max + 3 * std` (matches both line 1538 and the implementation).
    - The chosen Gap-2 resolution is applied; the four 47.6b.3.1 tests still pass with the new field name (or the new dual-field schema).
    - `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_fallback_to_filter_when_insufficient` has at least one new assertion on the `extras` count for the all-sentinel L1 case.
    - `cd scripts/stencil_gen && uv run pytest tests/test_bo.py -k test_clamp_sentinel_rows -x -q` → 4 passed.
    - No regression on `cd scripts/stencil_gen && uv run pytest tests/test_bo.py -x -q --deselect tests/test_bo.py::TestBranin --deselect tests/test_bo.py::TestBiasMisspec --deselect tests/test_bo.py::TestCostMisspec --deselect tests/test_bo.py::TestMultiModal`.
  - File: `scripts/stencil_gen/stencil_gen/bo.py`, `scripts/stencil_gen/tests/test_bo.py`
  - Test: `cd scripts/stencil_gen && uv run pytest tests/test_bo.py -k test_clamp_sentinel_rows -x -q`
  - **Done 2026-04-29.** All three gaps closed; took the recommended fix branch on each.
    - **Gap 1 (docstring formula):** changed `bo.py:1553` from `mean + 3 * std` to `max + 3 * std` so both formula references in the `clamp_sentinel_rows` docstring (`bo.py:1538` and `:1553`) match the implementation at `bo.py:1853-1855` (`fin_vals.max() + 3.0 * fin_vals.std(ddof=0)`). Also tightened the line 1553 commentary so the "constrained-BO via one-sided log-barrier" pattern reference correctly maps to the max-not-mean formula.
    - **Gap 2 (Option 1, rename + document):** renamed `extras["n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity"]` → `extras["n_sentinel_per_fidelity"]` in `bo.py:2206-2208` (variable also renamed `clamped_per_fid` → `sentinel_per_fid` for consistency) and updated the surrounding code-comment to spell out the treatment-agnostic semantics (clamped *and* fallback-filtered rows are tallied together; the field name reflects *occurrence* not *treatment*). The `clamp_sentinel_rows=True` docstring at `bo.py:1558-1563` got a new closing paragraph documenting the field name and pointing at this item; the `BOResult.extras` docstring at `bo.py:204-208` got a parenthetical describing both `n_sentinel_per_fidelity` (clamp-on path) and `n_sentinel_filtered` (clamp-off path). Two of the four 47.6b.3.1 tests pin the new key name (`test_clamp_sentinel_rows_default_true_on` and `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_false_preserves_filter_contract`); both updated in place. The other two tests (`_uses_per_fidelity_clamp` and `_fallback_to_filter_when_insufficient`) did not previously reference the field name so they did not need changes for the rename itself.
    - **Gap 3 (fallback-path extras assertion):** extended `test_clamp_sentinel_rows_fallback_to_filter_when_insufficient` to capture `result = run_mfbo(...)` (it previously discarded the return value) and added three new assertions: (i) `"n_sentinel_per_fidelity" in result.extras` (key present even on the fallback path — pins the Gap-2 semantics), (ii) `n_l1_in_history >= 1` (sanity check on the synthetic — init-design seeded at least one cheap row), (iii) `per_fid[1] == n_l1_in_history` (every L1 row in eval_history is recorded as a sentinel because the synthetic returns `_BO_SENTINEL` for every cheap eval — fallback-filtered rows ARE counted under the same key). The mutation acceptance criterion is met: a refactor that excluded fallback-filtered rows from the tally would make `per_fid[1]` strictly less than `n_l1_in_history`.
    - **No external consumers affected.** Per a 2026-04-29 grep audit, `n_sentinel_clamped_per_fidelity` was only referenced in `bo.py` and `test_bo.py` (no JSON payloads, no `_bo_io.py`, no docs, no other tests). The rename was strictly internal to the BO module and its test surface.
    - **Test result:** `pytest tests/test_bo.py -k test_clamp_sentinel_rows -x -q` → 4 passed in 19.17 s. Full `tests/test_bo.py` excluding slow validation classes (TestBranin/TestBiasMisspec/TestCostMisspec/TestMultiModal): 114 passed + 1 skipped + 4 deselected in 854.86 s (~14 min). Adjacent `tests/test_sweep_bo.py` → 31 passed in 4.12 s. No regressions on either suite.
    - **One deviation from the plan body's Gap-3 assertion target.** The plan body suggested asserting `per_fid[1] == 8` literally (the n_init L1 count from the DOE). The committed test asserts `per_fid[1] == n_l1_in_history` instead — exactly the same target, but computed dynamically from `result.eval_history`. Reason: the test's `budget_evals=14, n_init=8, hf_anchors=3, K=2` configuration admits acquisition iterations that the cost-aware utility may steer to L1 (depending on quota / variance-guard interactions — these are independent of the clamp mechanism), so the L1 row count can be `8` (init only) or larger (init + acquisition picks). Hardcoding `8` would silently couple the test to the cost-aware utility's HF/cheap split decisions. Computing the count from the eval history pins the right contract: "every L1 row was sentinel; every L1 sentinel was tallied" — independent of how many L1 picks the loop made.

- [x] **47.6b.3.2** Tracker for the basin-proximity gap closure on `TestMultiModal::test_classical_alpha_finds_a_basin` after 47.6b.3.1's clamp mechanism landed. The structural fix worked: `best_objective` is finite at 4/5 seeds (vs 0/5 pre-fix) and `_recommend_incumbent` no longer extrapolates into infeasible corners. But the basin-proximity contract `min(d_BL, d_DE) < 0.1` still misses (closest seed=3 at `d_BL=0.30`, `best_obj=0.15`). The per-seed measurement table is in 47.6b.3.1's Done note. **This item is split into 47.6b.3.2a → 47.6b.3.2d below for incremental delivery** — the 5-seed sweep at `budget_evals=60` is ~12 min wall time (consistent with the path (a) precedent in 47.3k.4d's two-Bash-invocation pattern), the candidate fixes (path b: Voronoi/UCB feasibility-aware recommendation, path c: threshold revision) are non-trivial, and the routing decision needs the path (a) measurement before it can be made. Each child item ships its measurement, mechanism, or routing decision independently. The tracker stays unchecked until the chosen path lands and the xfail is removed from `TestMultiModal`. The original scoping notes — three candidate fixes, recommendation order (a → b → c), acceptance criterion, Voronoi test sketches, and 47.6b.3.3 follow-up clause — are preserved verbatim below for context; each child references this body for the rich background.

  - **Pick one fix (in order of recommendation):**
    1. **(a) Bump `budget_evals` to 60.** Path (a) from 47.6b.3's empirical-fallback list was rejected on the unfixed pipeline (the variance guard / sentinel-collapse failure mode was structural, not budget-driven), but with 47.6b.3.1's clamp in place, the GP no longer wastes picks on infeasible corner regions. Doubling the budget gives the GP more HF coverage to localise the basins. **Pro:** zero machinery change; cheap to measure (~12 min for 5 seeds). **Con:** if (a) clears the bar, it sets the test's budget to 60 which conflicts with the rest of the 47.6b.3 contract (n_init=8, budget_evals=30); a revised 47.6b.3 docstring would document the deviation.
    2. **(b) Voronoi/UCB feasibility-aware recommendation.** Add a feasibility predicate to `_recommend_incumbent`: filter out grid points within some L2 radius of any recorded sentinel `x` (Voronoi mask), or use the upper-confidence-bound (UCB) of the posterior at each grid point instead of the mean (UCB penalises high-variance regions, which the clamped GP places at sentinel boundaries). **Pro:** addresses the residual extrapolation hazard at boundary regions; composes orthogonally with the clamp (the clamp keeps the GP fit healthy; UCB/Voronoi keeps the recommendation feasibility-aware). **Con:** more machinery; the Voronoi radius (or UCB beta) is another hyperparameter to tune.
    3. **(c) Revise the basin-proximity threshold from 0.1 to 0.4.** De-scoping option matching the routing-C precedent from 47.3k.4e (where the AugmentedBranin acceptance bar was de-scoped from `< 0.5` to `< 3.7` per the empirical floor). With the post-47.6b.3.1 empirical floor `d_BL=0.30`, a threshold of `0.4` would clear seeds 3 (d_BL=0.30), 4 (d_BL=0.39), and possibly 1 (d_BL=0.63) and 2 (d_BL=0.74) — but seed 0 (d_BL=1.39) would still miss. Per the 47.6b.3 plan body's "Do NOT silently relax the threshold" guidance, this option is acceptable only if (a) and (b) both fail.
  - Recommended: **(a) first** — cheapest to measure; if (a) clears ≥ 4/5 at `<0.1`, revise 47.6b.3's `budget_evals=30` to `budget_evals=60` and proceed. If (a) still misses, escalate to **(b)** with a Voronoi mask helper. Save **(c)** for the last-resort case where (a) and (b) both miss.
  - **Acceptance:** `pytest tests/test_bo.py -k TestMultiModal --run-slow` passes (xfail removed, ≥ 4/5 seeds find a basin at the chosen fix's threshold) AND `pytest tests/test_bo.py -k TestRunMFBO --run-slow` passes (no regression). Wall time ≤ 600 s for the multi-modal sweep with the chosen fix (path (a) at `budget_evals=60` may exceed the 600s cap; if so, raise the cap with a one-line note).
  - **Tests to add (under `TestRunMFBO`, only if path (b) is taken):**
    - `test_voronoi_recommendation_filters_sentinel_neighbours` — synthetic 2-fidelity with known sentinel cluster; with the Voronoi mechanism enabled, assert the recommendation lands outside the sentinel cluster (within some user-set radius).
    - `test_voronoi_recommendation_default_off_preserves_recommendation` — collapse-equivalence template; bytewise-identical recommendations between default-off and explicit-no-mask.
  - **Empirical fallback:** if all three paths miss the 4/5 bar, document the gap in a 47.6b.3.3 follow-up; the multi-modal coverage may be a fundamental limitation of single-shot MF-BO at small budgets and require restart strategies (multi-start MF-BO with N=3-5 independent loops, picking the best across loops). That is plan-48 territory.
  - File: `scripts/stencil_gen/stencil_gen/bo.py`, `scripts/stencil_gen/tests/test_bo.py`
  - Test: `cd scripts/stencil_gen && uv run pytest tests/test_bo.py -x -q -k "TestMultiModal" --run-slow`

    **Routing implication for 47.6b.3.2b:** path (a) decisively does NOT close the basin-proximity gap. Four of five seeds (0, 1, 2, 4) are bytewise-identical between budget=30 and budget=60 because BoTorch's `scipy_minimize` / `L-BFGS-B` marginal-likelihood optimiser terminates with status `ABNORMAL` early in the loop (well before the new budget headroom is consumed); the extra budget is unreachable. Seed 3 is the most damning data point: pre-fix it was the closest seed to BL (`d_BL=0.30`, `best_obj=0.15`); under path (a) with the same composition kwargs but doubled budget it lands at `(0.391, 0.095)` with `d_BL=1.17` — a ~4× regression away from any basin. The 39 HF evals at seed 3 means this seed actually consumed substantial budget, so the regression cannot be blamed on early `error` exit — it is a genuine basin-discovery failure under the cost-aware utility once enough HF coverage has been spent.

    **Routing decision (for 47.6b.3.2b to consume):** path (a) misses, so 47.6b.3.2b should open 47.6b.3.2c for path (b) (Voronoi/UCB feasibility-aware recommendation per the parent 47.6b.3.2 mechanism sketch). - [x] **47.6b.3.2.0** Plan-text fix (residual from 47.6b.3.2's split into 47.6b.3.2a–47.6b.3.2d): the UCB description in 47.6b.3.2c's "Mechanism sketch" step (3) is internally contradictory and contradicts the parent 47.6b.3.2's stated goal. Concretely, line 1542 reads "For `\"ucb\"`: replace the posterior-mean ranking with `mu - beta * sigma` (UCB lower-confidence bound; for minimisation, lower mu and lower sigma both win)" — but with score `mu - beta * sigma` and minimization (lowest score wins), HIGHER sigma actually wins (subtracting more sigma yields a lower score). That formula is the standard exploration-LCB acquisition (rewards high variance) — exactly the OPPOSITE of "penalises high-variance regions, which the clamped GP places at sentinel boundaries" (parent 47.6b.3.2 line 1509, the explicit mechanism goal). Three of four signals point at `mu + beta * sigma` (the parent goal "penalises high-variance"; 47.6b.3.2c's own prose "lower sigma wins"; 47.6b.3.1's clamp diagnosis where sentinel-boundary regions have BOTH high mu and high sigma — so adding sigma further inflates the score and they get avoided). Only the literal `mu - beta * sigma` formula contradicts. An implementer copying verbatim would build a recommendation that EXPLORES sentinel boundaries instead of avoiding them — exactly the regression 47.6b.3.2c is meant to close. **Plan-text-only fix** — no production code or tests to change here (this lands before 47.6b.3.2c is implemented, so there is no buggy implementation yet). Mirrors the 47.6b.0 / 47.6b.3.0 pattern. **Do this before starting 47.6b.3.2c (only blocks 47.6b.3.2c, not 47.6b.3.2a/47.6b.3.2b).**
  - **Fix:** in 47.6b.3.2c's "Mechanism sketch" step (3) (line 1542):
    1. Change the formula `mu - beta * sigma` → `mu + beta * sigma`.
    2. Replace the label "UCB lower-confidence bound" with "upper-confidence bound on the minimization target (the pessimistic estimate; lower mu wins, lower sigma wins — i.e. high-variance regions are penalised)".
    3. Keep the `ucb_beta: float = 2.0` default and the Auer et al. 2002 citation (the citation is for the bandit-maximization UCB `mu + beta * sigma`; the same formula applies here with the sign convention adjusted for minimization — i.e. the candidate with the lowest pessimistic upper-bound is preferred).
  - **Cross-reference:** the parent 47.6b.3.2's prose at line 1509 ("UCB penalises high-variance regions, which the clamped GP places at sentinel boundaries") is informally correct in intent but uses "UCB" loosely — leave that verbatim per the commit-1fa9aad preservation directive, but add a one-clause cross-reference inside 47.6b.3.2c's step (3) that points at the parent's prose as the authoritative goal statement (so a future implementer cannot rationalise the wrong sign by appealing to the LCB literature).
  - **Acceptance:** 47.6b.3.2c's step (3) at line 1542 now reads `mu + beta * sigma` (not `mu - beta * sigma`); a `grep -n 'mu - beta \* sigma' plans/47-mfbo.md` returns no hits in 47.6b.3.2c's body (this 47.6b.3.2.0 item itself is exempt — pedagogical context for the bug being fixed). The label "lower-confidence bound" is removed from 47.6b.3.2c (the only confidence-bound applicable to minimization here is the upper bound). The cross-reference to the parent's goal statement is present. Existing `tests/test_bo.py + tests/test_sweep_bo.py` suite untouched (no production-code change).

- [x] **47.6b.3.2c** Tracker for path (b) — Voronoi/UCB feasibility-aware recommendation on top of 47.6b.3.1's clamp. (The original "conditional, opens only if 47.6b.3.2b routes via the < 4/5 path because budget=60 alone misses" preface fired: 47.6b.3.2b's routing decision opened this item because 47.6b.3.2a's path-(a) measurement got 0/5 seeds passing `min(d_BL, d_DE) < 0.1` at `budget_evals=60` — see 47.6b.3.2b's Done note for the full routing rationale and 47.6b.3.2a's per-seed table for the empirical baseline this path is measured against.) **Prerequisite:** land 47.6b.3.2.0 (UCB sign-convention plan-text fix) before implementing the `"ucb"` strategy here so the formula in step (3) below is the upper-confidence bound `mu + beta * sigma` (penalises high-variance regions per the parent 47.6b.3.2 goal at line 1509). Add a feasibility predicate to `_recommend_incumbent`: filter out grid points within some L2 radius of any recorded sentinel `x` (Voronoi mask), or use the upper-confidence-bound (UCB) of the posterior at each grid point instead of the mean (UCB penalises high-variance regions, which the clamped GP places at sentinel boundaries). The clamp landed by 47.6b.3.1 keeps the GP fit healthy; UCB/Voronoi keeps the recommendation feasibility-aware. The empirical-fallback baseline for this path is 47.6b.3.2a's per-seed table (so the comparison is "with vs without UCB/Voronoi at budget=60"; if budget=60 alone got 2/5, this path needs to lift to ≥ 4/5). **This item is split into 47.6b.3.2c.1 → 47.6b.3.2c.4 below for incremental delivery** — the parent's ~50–90 min wall-time estimate (30–60 min implementation + 12 min real-cascade re-run + 10 min unit tests) exceeds a single Ralph cycle's 10-min Bash timeout per command, so each child ships its mechanism + unit tests independently with the existing `tests/test_bo.py + tests/test_sweep_bo.py` suite green; 47.6b.3.2c.4 runs the multi-modal regression sweep and routes to acceptance (xfail removal) or 47.6b.3.2d. The original mechanism sketch, test list, acceptance criterion, and wall-time estimate are preserved verbatim below for context; each child references this body for the rich background. The tracker stays unchecked until 47.6b.3.2c.4 completes.
  - **Mechanism sketch:**
    1. Add `recommendation_strategy: str = "mean"` keyword-only param to `run_mfbo` (default `"mean"` reproduces pre-47.6b.3.2c behaviour). Options: `"mean"`, `"voronoi"`, `"ucb"`. The dispatch lives inside `_recommend_incumbent` so the keyword threads through cleanly.
    2. For `"voronoi"`: pass the sentinel `x` history into `_recommend_incumbent`; filter out grid points within `voronoi_radius` (new kwarg, default `0.1`) of any sentinel point. Reject the grid candidate if it falls inside the Voronoi cell of a sentinel; pick the lowest-mean candidate among the survivors.
    3. For `"ucb"`: replace the posterior-mean ranking with `mu + beta * sigma` (upper-confidence bound on the minimization target — the pessimistic estimate; lower mu wins, lower sigma wins, so high-variance regions are penalised). This matches the parent 47.6b.3.2's stated goal at line 1509 ("UCB penalises high-variance regions, which the clamped GP places at sentinel boundaries"); the parent is the authoritative goal statement and the formula here is the literal mechanism that satisfies it. New kwarg `ucb_beta: float = 2.0` (Auer et al. 2002 standard for the bandit-maximization UCB `mu + beta * sigma`; the same formula applies here with the sign convention adjusted for minimization — i.e. the candidate with the lowest pessimistic upper-bound is preferred).
    4. Either path: must compose with the clamp from 47.6b.3.1 — verify the GP `posterior()` call uses the clamped Y_train (already the case post-47.6b.3.1; just sanity-check via a unit test).
  - **Tests to add (under `TestRunMFBO`):**
    - `test_voronoi_recommendation_filters_sentinel_neighbours` — synthetic 2-fidelity with known sentinel cluster; with the Voronoi mechanism enabled, assert the recommendation lands outside the sentinel cluster (within some user-set radius).
    - `test_voronoi_recommendation_default_off_preserves_recommendation` — collapse-equivalence template (mirrors 47.3j.1 / 47.3j.2 / 47.3k.3): default `"mean"` vs explicit `"mean"` must produce bytewise-identical recommendations. Catches a refactor that breaks the default short-circuit.
    - `test_ucb_recommendation_default_off_preserves_recommendation` — same shape for the UCB strategy: default `"mean"` vs explicit `"mean"` bytewise-identical.
    - `test_recommendation_strategy_validates_choices` — parametrised over `["foo", "", None]`, all raise `ValueError(match="recommendation_strategy")`.
  - **Acceptance:** if path (b) clears ≥ 4/5 seeds at `< 0.1` on the 47.6b.3.2a baseline (re-measure with the new strategy enabled), declare 47.6b.3.2 done by removing the xfail on `TestMultiModal`, updating its budget if needed, and marking 47.6b.3.2 `[x]`. If path (b) still misses, open 47.6b.3.2d for path (c) threshold revision (last resort).

- [x] **47.6b.3.2c.0** Plan-text fix (residual from 47.6b.3.2c's split into 47.6b.3.2c.1–47.6b.3.2c.4, filed in the 2026-04-29 review of 29aa406): two child items misdescribe the existing code surface they extend, and an implementer copying verbatim would either build against a phantom `_recommend_incumbent` signature (47.6b.3.2c.1) or use an inconsistent sentinel-row filter against the existing 47.3b finite-mask convention (47.6b.3.2c.2). **Plan-text-only fix** — no production code, no tests; mirrors the 47.6b.0 / 47.6b.3.0 / 47.6b.3.2.0 pattern. **Do this before starting 47.6b.3.2c.1.**
  - **Issue 1 (47.6b.3.2c.1: phantom helper signature in the Mechanism paragraph):** the Mechanism paragraph currently claims "the helper currently takes `model, train_X, train_Y, target_fid_idx, d, bounds_t, seed`". The actual `_recommend_incumbent` signature in `scripts/stencil_gen/stencil_gen/bo.py:1175` is `(model, bounds, target_fidelity_index, d, seed, *, n_grid=1024)` — `train_X` and `train_Y` are NOT existing parameters of this helper (those names live on `_compute_hf_uncertainty_signal` at `bo.py:1210`, a different helper). The two existing call sites in `run_mfbo` (`bo.py:1950` and `bo.py:2156`) pass `(final_model, bounds_t, target_fid_idx, d, seed)`. An implementer copying the c.1 mechanism verbatim would either (a) hallucinate `train_X`/`train_Y` parameters and break the call sites, or (b) discover the inconsistency mid-implementation and pause. **Fix:** rewrite the parenthetical to `(the helper currently takes `(model, bounds, target_fidelity_index, d, seed, *, n_grid=1024)`; the existing call sites pass `(final_model, bounds_t, target_fid_idx, d, seed)`)`. The `"mean"` branch staying bytewise-identical clause is unaffected.
  - **Issue 2 (47.6b.3.2c.2: inconsistent sentinel-row filter between header and Mechanism):** the c.2 item header currently says sentinel rows are "recorded in `eval_history` as `BOEval` rows where `value == _BO_SENTINEL`"; the Mechanism paragraph says "filter by `value >= _BO_SENTINEL/2` per the existing 47.3b sentinel-detection convention". These two filters disagree, and the strict-equality form (`== _BO_SENTINEL`) is strictly weaker — it would miss sentinel rows produced by user-injected synthetic `objective=` callbacks that return NaN/inf (e.g. the `test_voronoi_recommendation_filters_sentinel_neighbours` test in c.2 itself injects a fake objective that could return any sentinel value). The actual existing convention in `bo.py:1818` and `bo.py:1855` is the finite-mask `np.isfinite(e.value) and e.value < _BO_SENTINEL / 2`; sentinel rows are its inverse, `not np.isfinite(e.value) or e.value >= _BO_SENTINEL/2`. **Fix:** rewrite the c.2 header parenthetical from "(recorded in `eval_history` as `BOEval` rows where `value == _BO_SENTINEL`)" to "(recorded in `eval_history` as `BOEval` rows that fail the existing finite-mask `np.isfinite(e.value) and e.value < _BO_SENTINEL / 2` per the 47.3b sentinel-detection convention)" so the header and Mechanism agree exactly. The Mechanism paragraph's filter description is correct as written and stays.
  - **Acceptance:** 47.6b.3.2c.1's Mechanism paragraph describes the correct `_recommend_incumbent` signature (no `train_X`/`train_Y` mentions); 47.6b.3.2c.2's header and Mechanism use the same sentinel-row filter (matching the existing finite-mask convention in `bo.py:1818`/`1855`). A `grep -n 'train_X, train_Y' plans/47-mfbo.md` returns no hits in 47.6b.3.2c.1's body (this 47.6b.3.2c.0 item itself is exempt — pedagogical context for the bug being fixed). A `grep -n 'value == _BO_SENTINEL' plans/47-mfbo.md` returns no hits in 47.6b.3.2c.2's body (same exemption). - [x] **47.6b.3.2c.1** Plumbing: add the `recommendation_strategy` kwarg surface + dispatch + validation + default-off equivalence. Pure plumbing — `"voronoi"` and `"ucb"` strategies raise `NotImplementedError("recommendation_strategy='voronoi' lands in 47.6b.3.2c.2")` (or `.3` for ucb) until 47.6b.3.2c.2 / 47.6b.3.2c.3 land their respective mechanisms. Splits 47.6b.3.2c step (1) of the mechanism sketch into its own item so the dispatch surface is exercised independently of the strategy implementations; mirrors the helper-extraction precedent from 47.3k.1.1 / 47.3j.2 (pure-helper unit tests catch mutations that integration tests miss).
  - **Mechanism (mirrors parent 47.6b.3.2c step (1) verbatim):** Add `recommendation_strategy: str = "mean"` keyword-only param to `run_mfbo` (positioned right after `clamp_sentinel_rows`, mirroring the layered "first warmup, then quota, then floor, then schedule, then bonus, then clamp, then recommendation" docstring ordering). Validate at the top of `run_mfbo` (alongside the other kwarg validators): `recommendation_strategy in {"mean", "voronoi", "ucb"}`, else raise `ValueError(match="recommendation_strategy")`. Thread the kwarg into `_recommend_incumbent` via a new positional/keyword argument (the helper currently takes `(model, bounds, target_fidelity_index, d, seed, *, n_grid=1024)`; the existing call sites pass `(final_model, bounds_t, target_fid_idx, d, seed)`); add `strategy: str = "mean"` and a top-of-function dispatch `if strategy == "mean": ...; elif strategy == "voronoi": raise NotImplementedError(...); elif strategy == "ucb": raise NotImplementedError(...)`. The `"mean"` branch is bytewise-identical to the pre-47.6b.3.2c body (literally lift the existing logic into the `"mean"` branch). 47.6b.3.2c.2 / 47.6b.3.2c.3 will replace the NotImplementedError stubs with the actual mechanism.
  - **Tests to add (under `TestRunMFBO`):**
    - `test_recommendation_strategy_validates_choices` (parent 47.6b.3.2c test 4) — parametrised over `["foo", "", None, "MEAN"]`, all raise `ValueError(match="recommendation_strategy")`. The case-sensitivity check (`"MEAN"`) catches a mutation that lower-cases the kwarg or accepts case-insensitive matches.
    - `test_recommendation_strategy_default_off_preserves_recommendation_collapse` — collapse-equivalence template (mirrors 47.3j.1 / 47.3j.2 / 47.3k.3.1 default-off pattern). Two runs with identical kwargs except `recommendation_strategy=None` (default → `"mean"`) and `recommendation_strategy="mean"` (explicit) must produce bytewise-identical `best_x`, `best_objective`, `stop_reason`, and `n_evals_per_fidelity`. Both branches traverse the new dispatch logic (the explicit `"mean"` path calls into the new dispatch even though it lands at the same code as default), so this catches a mutation that changes the dispatch behaviour from the default path.
    - `test_recommendation_strategy_voronoi_raises_not_implemented` — pin the stub: explicit `recommendation_strategy="voronoi"` raises `NotImplementedError(match="47.6b.3.2c.2")`. When 47.6b.3.2c.2 lands and the stub is replaced, this test should be deleted (and the deletion is the natural point at which 47.6b.3.2c.2's voronoi-mechanism tests are added).
    - `test_recommendation_strategy_ucb_raises_not_implemented` — same shape: `recommendation_strategy="ucb"` raises `NotImplementedError(match="47.6b.3.2c.3")`. Deleted when 47.6b.3.2c.3 lands.

- [x] **47.6b.3.2c.2** Implement the `"voronoi"` strategy on top of 47.6b.3.2c.1's plumbing. Replaces the `NotImplementedError` stub for `recommendation_strategy="voronoi"` in `_recommend_incumbent` with the actual Voronoi mask. Threads sentinel `x` history from `run_mfbo`'s loop (recorded in `eval_history` as `BOEval` rows that fail the existing finite-mask `np.isfinite(e.value) and e.value < _BO_SENTINEL / 2` per the 47.3b sentinel-detection convention) into the helper. New kwarg `voronoi_radius: float = 0.1` validated `> 0` and finite. Per-strategy unit tests pin the mechanism behaviour.
  - **Mechanism (mirrors parent 47.6b.3.2c step (2) verbatim):** **Step (0): delete the eager `if recommendation_strategy == "voronoi": raise NotImplementedError(...)` line from `run_mfbo` (currently `bo.py:1724-1727`; added by 47.6b.3.2c.1 to surface the stub before the BO loop's `except Exception:` wrapper at `bo.py:2061` swallows it; with the helper's `"voronoi"` branch now implementing the real mechanism, the eager raise must go so the new code path is reached).** Then: in `_recommend_incumbent`'s `"voronoi"` branch, accept the sentinel `x` history as a new helper kwarg (`sentinel_x: np.ndarray | None = None`, shape `(n_sentinel, d)`). Compute pairwise L2 distances from each Sobol' grid point to every sentinel `x`; mask out grid points where `min_distance < voronoi_radius`. If all grid points are masked (degenerate sentinel cluster covers the whole bounded region), fall back to the unmasked posterior-mean argmin and log a warning via `extras["voronoi_fallback"] = True`. Pick the lowest-mean candidate among the survivors. `run_mfbo` collects sentinel `x` history from `eval_history` (filter by `value >= _BO_SENTINEL/2` per the existing 47.3b sentinel-detection convention) and passes it to `_recommend_incumbent` when `recommendation_strategy == "voronoi"`. Validation: `voronoi_radius > 0` and finite, else `ValueError(match="voronoi_radius")`. Default `0.1` per the parent body; tunable per call.
  - **Tests to add / update (under `TestRunMFBO`):**
    - **Delete** `test_recommendation_strategy_voronoi_raises_not_implemented` (from 47.6b.3.2c.1) — the stub is replaced by the real mechanism.

Pin: this test must FAIL if the Voronoi mask is removed from the helper (e.g. mutation that returns the unmasked argmin even in `"voronoi"` mode).
    - `test_voronoi_recommendation_default_off_preserves_recommendation` (parent 47.6b.3.2c test 2) — collapse-equivalence template: `recommendation_strategy="mean"` vs `recommendation_strategy="voronoi", voronoi_radius=1e-30` (radius so small that no grid point is masked) must produce bytewise-identical recommendations on a synthetic with no sentinel rows. Pins: the voronoi branch is a strict superset of the mean branch when `voronoi_radius → 0`; mutations that change the default mean-branch behaviour are caught.
    - `test_voronoi_radius_validates_range` — parametrised over `[0.0, -0.1, NaN, inf, -inf]`, all raise `ValueError(match="voronoi_radius")`.

Assert `result.extras["voronoi_fallback"] is True` and the recommendation is finite (falls back to unmasked argmin). Pins: the degenerate case does not crash the loop.

  - **Done 2026-04-29.** Step (0) executed first: deleted the eager `if recommendation_strategy == "voronoi": raise NotImplementedError(...)` block from `run_mfbo` (`bo.py:1724-1727` pre-fix); the eager stub for `"ucb"` stays per 47.6b.3.2c.3's Step (0) instruction. Added `voronoi_radius: float = 0.1` kwarg to `run_mfbo` (positioned right after `recommendation_strategy`, mirroring the layered docstring ordering); validation rejects NaN, `<= 0`, and non-finite (inf/-inf) with `ValueError(match="voronoi_radius")` and runs unconditionally so the kwarg surface is sound regardless of strategy choice. Replaced the `NotImplementedError` stub for `"voronoi"` in `_recommend_incumbent` with the actual mask: the same Sobol' grid + posterior-mean ranking as `"mean"`, with grid points within `voronoi_radius` (L2) of any sentinel `x` excluded via `torch.where(feasible_mask, mean, +inf)`. When all grid points fall inside the union of Voronoi cells, the helper falls back to the unmasked `argmin(mean)` and signals the fallback by setting `info_out["voronoi_fallback"] = True` (passed in by `run_mfbo` for the final-recommendation call only; the in-loop variance-guard call passes `info_out=None` since the mid-loop fallback is not surfaced).
  - **Plumbing additions:** added a small pure helper `_collect_sentinel_x(eval_history) -> np.ndarray | None` that filters `eval_history` by the inverse of the existing 47.3b finite-mask convention (`np.isfinite(e.value) and e.value < _BO_SENTINEL / 2`) — exactly the predicate cross-referenced in 47.6b.3.2c.0's Issue 2 fix. Returns a fresh `(n_sentinel, d)` numpy array or `None` when no sentinels exist (helper masking branch then no-ops). Threaded sentinel_x + voronoi_radius into both `_recommend_incumbent` call sites (in-loop variance guard at `bo.py:~2075` + final recommendation at `bo.py:~2226`); the final call additionally passes a fresh `info_out` dict that is checked after the call and merged into `extras_payload` as `extras["voronoi_fallback"] = True` when the fallback fired.
  - **Tests** (4 new + 1 deletion, all in `TestRunMFBO`, replacing the 47.6b.3.2c.1 stub `test_recommendation_strategy_voronoi_raises_not_implemented`):
    - `test_voronoi_recommendation_filters_sentinel_neighbours` — synthetic 2-fidelity injecting sentinels for `||x|| < 0.3` plus an underlying objective `norm(x)` whose unmasked minimum sits at the disk boundary; with `voronoi_radius=0.45`, asserts `norm(best_x) >= radius - max_sentinel_norm = 0.45 - 0.3 = 0.15` so the mask's effect is unambiguous. Catches a mutation that drops the masking branch or returns the unmasked argmin in `"voronoi"` mode.
    - `test_voronoi_recommendation_default_off_preserves_recommendation` — collapse-equivalence template: `recommendation_strategy="mean"` vs `recommendation_strategy="voronoi", voronoi_radius=1e-30` (no point can be within 1e-30 of any sentinel, so masking is empirically a no-op). Pins bytewise-identical `best_x` (`atol=1e-9`), `best_objective`, `stop_reason`, and `n_evals_per_fidelity`. Mirrors the 47.3j.1 / 47.3j.2 / 47.3k.3 default-off pattern. Also asserts `voronoi_fallback` is absent in both extras dicts (mean strategy never sets it; voronoi strategy with `radius=1e-30` never enters the all-masked branch).
    - `test_voronoi_radius_validates_range` — parametrised over `[0.0, -0.1, NaN, inf, -inf]`, all raise `ValueError(match="voronoi_radius")`. Extended past the plan body's `[0.0, -0.1, NaN]` to also cover `inf` / `-inf` since `np.isfinite()` catches them too.
    - `test_voronoi_fallback_when_all_grid_points_masked` — synthetic with `voronoi_radius=10.0` (much larger than the box's diagonal `2*sqrt(2)≈2.83`), so any single sentinel covers the entire grid. Asserts `result.extras["voronoi_fallback"] is True` AND the recommendation remains finite AND in-bounds. Pins: the degenerate case does not crash the loop.
    - **Deleted** `test_recommendation_strategy_voronoi_raises_not_implemented` per the plan body's "Delete the stub test" instruction.
  - **Three deviations from the plan body worth flagging for 47.6b.3.2c.3 / 47.6b.3.2c.4:**
    - **`info_out` kwarg pattern instead of return-tuple.** The plan body sketched the helper as setting `info_out` directly. Implemented it as an optional mutable kwarg on `_recommend_incumbent` (default `None` — no-op for callers that don't care about the fallback flag). Cleaner than changing the helper's return type from `np.ndarray` to `tuple[np.ndarray, dict]` (which would have broken the in-loop variance-guard call site that doesn't care about the flag). The in-loop call passes `info_out=None`; only the final-recommendation call passes a fresh dict and merges its content into `extras_payload`. 47.6b.3.2c.3 (UCB) does not need the `info_out` dict — UCB has no fallback path — so the kwarg stays optional and defaults to `None`.
    - **`_collect_sentinel_x` helper extracted (not inlined).** The plan body's "filter `eval_history` by [the finite-mask predicate]" could have been inlined at each call site, but the same logic appears at three places in `bo.py` (variance guard, final recommendation, sentinel-clamp tally) — extracting the helper keeps the predicate in one place and matches the precedent set by `_resolve_min_acq_iters` (47.3k.1.1) / `_stagnation_triggered` (47.3e) / `_variance_guard_relative_fired` (47.3k.2.1). The helper does NOT replace the inline filter at the existing tally site (`bo.py:~2284`) because that loop also needs to count by fidelity — refactoring that for ~6 lines of shared filter-logic would have unnecessary churn. 47.6b.3.2c.4's empirical re-measurement should not need to re-derive sentinel filtering — it can `from stencil_gen.bo import _collect_sentinel_x` directly if needed.
    - **Variance-guard's in-loop `_recommend_incumbent` call also threads `sentinel_x`.** The plan body did not explicitly say this; the natural interpretation is that the strategy applies uniformly (both call sites use the same `recommendation_strategy`). With `recommendation_strategy="voronoi"`, the in-loop incumbent recommendation also avoids sentinel regions — which is exactly what we want when the variance guard checks "is the incumbent well-localised?" (we don't want the guard to fire when the incumbent is at an infeasible point). The in-loop call wraps in `try/except Exception:` already, so any voronoi-related failure (e.g. all-masked fallback) silently skips the variance check that iteration without aborting the loop. The 47.6b.3.2c.4 multi-modal re-measurement should observe the in-loop voronoi behaviour as a side effect — sentinel-rich runs are less likely to early-exit on variance.
  - **Test result:** `pytest tests/test_bo.py -k "test_voronoi or test_recommendation_strategy"` → 14 passed in 83 s (5 voronoi mechanism + 5 existing recommendation_strategy + 4 ucb stub + 1 default-off-collapse). Full `tests/test_bo.py` excluding slow validation classes (TestBranin / TestBiasMisspec / TestCostMisspec / TestMultiModal): 128 passed + 1 skipped + 4 deselected in 950 s (~16 min). `tests/test_sweep_bo.py` → 31 passed in 4.25 s. No regressions on either suite.
  - **Implication for 47.6b.3.2c.3:** the `"ucb"` strategy can now be implemented in `_recommend_incumbent` without the `sentinel_x` / `voronoi_radius` plumbing burden — those kwargs are already on the helper signature and the UCB branch ignores them. UCB needs to query `model.posterior(...).variance` (not just `.mean`); the helper currently only reads `.mean`, so 47.6b.3.2c.3 will need to add a `.variance` query inside the `"ucb"` branch only. The eager `if recommendation_strategy == "ucb": raise NotImplementedError(...)` at `bo.py:1816-1819` [corrected by 47.6b.3.2c.2.0 from the original (incorrect) `bo.py:1733-1736`] is still in place per the c.1.0 Step (0) instruction, and 47.6b.3.2c.3's Step (0) deletes it.

- [x] **47.6b.3.2c.3** Implement the `"ucb"` strategy on top of 47.6b.3.2c.1's plumbing. Replaces the `NotImplementedError` stub for `recommendation_strategy="ucb"` in `_recommend_incumbent` with the upper-confidence-bound ranking `mu + beta * sigma` per the parent 47.6b.3.2c step (3) (post-47.6b.3.2.0 sign convention). New kwarg `ucb_beta: float = 2.0` validated `>= 0` and finite (`0` collapses to mean-only ranking — useful as a no-op for the default-off contract). Per-strategy unit test pins the mechanism behaviour.
  - **Mechanism (mirrors parent 47.6b.3.2c step (3) verbatim, post-47.6b.3.2.0 sign fix):** **Step (0): delete the eager `if recommendation_strategy == "ucb": raise NotImplementedError(...)` line from `run_mfbo` (currently `bo.py:1816-1819`; same rationale as 47.6b.3.2c.2's Step (0) — the in-loop variance-guard's `except Exception:` wrapper at `bo.py:2172` would otherwise swallow the stub's `NotImplementedError`, but the new mechanism in this branch must be reached unconditionally).** Then: in `_recommend_incumbent`'s `"ucb"` branch, query the GP's posterior `mean` AND `variance` at each Sobol' grid point at `target_fid_idx` (the helper currently only reads `mean`). Compute `sigma = torch.sqrt(variance.clamp(min=0.0))` (clamp protects against tiny negative variances from numerical roundoff in BoTorch's posterior chain). Score each grid point as `score = mean + ucb_beta * sigma` (upper-confidence bound on the minimization target — the pessimistic estimate; lower mu wins, lower sigma wins). Pick the grid point with the lowest score. Validation: `ucb_beta >= 0` and finite, else `ValueError(match="ucb_beta")`. Default `2.0` per the parent body (Auer et al. 2002 standard, applied here with the sign convention adjusted for minimization per 47.6b.3.2.0).
  - **Tests to add / update (under `TestRunMFBO`):**
    - **Delete** `test_recommendation_strategy_ucb_raises_not_implemented` (from 47.6b.3.2c.1) — the stub is replaced by the real mechanism.
    - `test_ucb_recommendation_default_off_preserves_recommendation` (parent 47.6b.3.2c test 3) — collapse-equivalence template: `recommendation_strategy="mean"` vs `recommendation_strategy="ucb", ucb_beta=0.0` (UCB collapses to mean-only when β=0) must produce bytewise-identical recommendations. Pins: the UCB branch is a strict generalisation of the mean branch when `ucb_beta → 0`; mutations that change the default mean-branch behaviour or the UCB formula's collapse property are caught (e.g. `mean - beta * sigma` would still produce bytewise-identical results at β=0, so this test alone does NOT catch the sign mutation — see the next test).
    - `test_ucb_recommendation_penalises_high_variance` (mutation-catcher for the sign convention) — synthetic where the GP posterior has two near-equal-mean candidates with very different variances (e.g. 1024-pt grid where one region is well-explored and another is sparsely-explored). With `ucb_beta=5.0` (aggressive), assert the recommendation lands in the well-explored (low-variance) region, NOT the sparsely-explored (high-variance) region. This test must FAIL under the mutation `score = mean - beta * sigma` (which would prefer the high-variance region — the LCB exploration acquisition the parent 47.6b.3.2.0 explicitly rejected). Pins the sign convention from the production code, not just from the docstring.
    - `test_ucb_beta_validates_range` — parametrised over `[-0.1, NaN, inf, -inf]`, all raise `ValueError(match="ucb_beta")`. (`0.0` is accepted per the no-op contract.)
  - **Acceptance:** `pytest tests/test_bo.py -k "test_ucb" --run-slow` → 3 passed (default-off + penalises-high-variance + beta validation). The deleted `_raises_not_implemented` test does not appear in the test file. Full `tests/test_bo.py` (excluding slow validation classes) green.
  - **Wall-time estimate:** ~20-30 min implementation + ~5 min for the 3 unit tests; well under the 10-min Bash timeout.
  - File: `scripts/stencil_gen/stencil_gen/bo.py`, `scripts/stencil_gen/tests/test_bo.py`
  - Test: `cd scripts/stencil_gen && uv run pytest tests/test_bo.py -x -q -k "TestRunMFBO and (test_ucb or test_recommendation_strategy_default_off)"`
  - **Done 2026-04-29.** Step (0) executed first: deleted the eager `if recommendation_strategy == "ucb": raise NotImplementedError(...)` block from `run_mfbo` (was at `bo.py:1816-1819` per 47.6b.3.2c.2.0). Added `ucb_beta: float = 2.0` kwarg to `run_mfbo` (positioned right after `voronoi_radius`, mirroring the layered docstring ordering); validation rejects negative, NaN, and non-finite (inf/-inf) values with `ValueError(match="ucb_beta")` and runs unconditionally so the kwarg surface is sound regardless of strategy choice. `0.0` is accepted (no-op contract for the default-off equivalence test). Replaced the `NotImplementedError` stub for `"ucb"` in `_recommend_incumbent` (also lifted from the helper's strategy validator — `"ucb"` is now in the `("mean", "voronoi", "ucb")` accepted set, with the `NotImplementedError` raise removed): the same Sobol' grid as `"mean"`/`"voronoi"`, but the score is `mean + ucb_beta * sigma` where `sigma = sqrt(variance.clamp(min=0.0))` (clamp protects against tiny negative variances from numerical roundoff in BoTorch's posterior chain — verified empirically: GPyTorch emits `NumericalWarning: Negative variance values detected` on near-singular kernels, the clamp absorbs them). The argmin is taken over `score` (the `voronoi` mask branch reads from the `score` variable too, so `ucb` composes cleanly with `voronoi` if both are ever combined — tested implicitly by the shared `score` variable name; no production combination today). Threaded `ucb_beta` into both `_recommend_incumbent` call sites (in-loop variance-guard at `bo.py:~2128` + final recommendation at `bo.py:~2346`), mirroring the 47.6b.3.2c.2 voronoi plumbing precedent.
  - **Tests** (3 new + 1 deletion, all in `TestRunMFBO`, replacing the 47.6b.3.2c.1 stub `test_recommendation_strategy_ucb_raises_not_implemented`):
    - `test_ucb_recommendation_default_off_preserves_recommendation` — collapse-equivalence template: `recommendation_strategy="ucb", ucb_beta=0.0` produces bytewise-identical `best_x`, `best_objective`, `stop_reason`, `n_evals_per_fidelity` to the `"mean"` strategy. Mirrors the 47.3j.1 / 47.3j.2 / 47.3k.3 default-off pattern. Catches mutations that change the formula's collapse property (e.g. `score = mean + ucb_beta * sigma + epsilon` would fail at β=0).
    - `test_ucb_recommendation_penalises_high_variance` — sign-convention mutation-catcher. Builds a 30-pt synthetic GP with data clustered near origin (well-explored, low variance there; high variance at corners) and calls `_recommend_incumbent` directly with `strategy="ucb", ucb_beta=5.0`. Asserts `||x_ucb|| < 1.0` (well inside the box). Under the WRONG sign mutation (`score = mean - beta * sigma`), the argmin would prefer the high-variance corners and `||x_ucb||` would tend toward `sqrt(2) ≈ 1.41` — the test reliably catches this. Pins the sign convention from the production code, not just from the docstring (mirrors the 47.3k.2.1 helper-extraction precedent: the test pins what a docstring cannot).
    - `test_ucb_beta_validates_range` — parametrised over `[-0.1, NaN, inf, -inf]`, all raise `ValueError(match="ucb_beta")`. `0.0` is accepted (the no-op-collapse path is verified by the `_default_off` test).
    - **Deleted** `test_recommendation_strategy_ucb_raises_not_implemented` per the plan body's "Delete the stub test" instruction.
  - **Two deviations from the plan body worth flagging for 47.6b.3.2c.4:**
    - **The `_recommend_incumbent` strategy validator was simplified** from `if strategy == "ucb": raise NotImplementedError(...); if strategy not in ("mean", "voronoi"): raise ValueError(...)` to a single `if strategy not in ("mean", "voronoi", "ucb"): raise ValueError(...)` — `"ucb"` is now in the accepted set. This is the natural consequence of deleting the stub: the validator no longer needs the special-case branch.
    - **`test_ucb_recommendation_penalises_high_variance` invokes `_recommend_incumbent` directly** (rather than running the full `run_mfbo` loop). The plan body sketch said "synthetic 100x-cost objective with two regions of similar mean but different variances", but that requires running the loop long enough for the GP to acquire enough HF picks at the centre and not the corners — fragile across BoTorch tuning. The direct-helper-call shape is cleaner: it builds a hand-crafted GP with known centre-vs-corner variance asymmetry and tests the helper's argmin behaviour directly. Same mutation-catching contract; smaller surface area for non-determinism. Mirrors the helper-extraction precedent from 47.3k.1.1 / 47.3j.2.
  - **Test result:** `pytest tests/test_bo.py -k "TestRunMFBO and (test_ucb or test_recommendation_strategy_default_off)"` → 7 passed in 58.5 s (3 new UCB tests with parametrise expansion = 6 effective, plus the existing `test_recommendation_strategy_default_off_preserves_recommendation_collapse`). Broader `pytest tests/test_bo.py -k "test_recommendation_strategy or test_voronoi or test_ucb"` → 19 passed in 111.6 s (5 strategy-validation + 4 voronoi mechanism + 3 default-off + 7 ucb mechanism). Full `TestRunMFBO + TestStagnationGuard + TestResolveMinAcqIters + TestVarianceGuardRelative + TestAcquisition` superset (excluding slow validation classes): 61 passed, 77 deselected in 963.53 s (~16 min). No regressions on either suite.

The 47.6b tracker's pointer flips to 47.6b.3.2d. - [x] **47.6b.3.2c.4b** Run the voronoi-strategy sweep at the default `voronoi_radius=0.1` on the same E4-classical real-cascade scaffold from 47.6b.3.2a. 5 seeds × 1 strategy at `budget_evals=60`. Mirrors 47.6b.3.2a's measurement-only shape; uses the harness extended in 47.6b.3.2c.4a.

  - **Done 2026-04-29.** Voronoi-strategy sweep complete; per-seed Markdown table below. Per the harness extended in 47.6b.3.2c.4a, ran two Bash invocations (`--seeds 0 1 2 --budget-evals 60` then `--seeds 3 4 --budget-evals 60`) with `--recommendation-strategy voronoi --voronoi-radius 0.1`. Total wall time **474 s (~7.9 min)**, well under the 12-min plan estimate (and consistent with 47.6b.3.2a's 7.8 min/5-seed baseline — the voronoi mask's per-grid-point distance computation overhead is empirically negligible vs the GP-fit/qMFKG cost).

    | seed | best_x | best_obj | d_BL | d_DE | found | stop_reason | n_HF | elapsed_s |
    |-----:|:-------|---------:|-----:|-----:|:-----:|:-----------:|-----:|----------:|
    | 0 | (0.460, 0.813)  | 1.00e+12 | 1.395 | 1.931 | False | error |  10 |  16.0 |
    | 1 | (-0.865, 0.786) | 6.612    | 0.631 | 0.727 | False | error |  14 |  17.7 |
    | 2 | (-0.680, 0.901) | 8.391    | 0.744 | 0.942 | False | error |  25 |  60.2 |
    | 3 | (0.391, 0.095)  | 1.643    | 1.167 | 1.801 | False | error |  39 | 373.1 |
    | 4 | (-0.433, 0.350) | 2.491    | 0.388 | 0.968 | False | error |   8 |   6.7 |

    **Pass count `min(d_BL, d_DE) < 0.1`: 0/5** (vs the required ≥ 4/5).

    **Per-seed comparison vs the 47.6b.3.2a baseline (mean strategy, budget=60, 0/5 pass):**

    | seed | mean baseline (47.6b.3.2a) `(d_BL, d_DE, best_obj)` | voronoi (this item) `(d_BL, d_DE, best_obj)` | trajectory |
    |-----:|---|---|---|
    | 0 | (1.395, 1.931, 1.00e+12) | (1.395, 1.931, 1.00e+12) | bytewise-identical |
    | 1 | (0.631, 0.727, 6.6123)   | (0.631, 0.727, 6.612)    | bytewise-identical |
    | 2 | (0.744, 0.942, 8.3914)   | (0.744, 0.942, 8.391)    | bytewise-identical |
    | 3 | (1.167, 1.801, 1.6428)   | (1.167, 1.801, 1.643)    | bytewise-identical |
    | 4 | (0.388, 0.968, 2.4914)   | (0.388, 0.968, 2.491)    | bytewise-identical |

    All 5 seeds bytewise-identical to the mean-strategy baseline (modulo `%g`-format trailing-digit rounding from the harness's `:.4g` `best_obj` print spec). The voronoi mask did NOT change the recommendation on any seed at this scaffold + budget. Two structural reasons:
    1. **Early `error` exit on every seed.** All 5 seeds terminate with `stop_reason="error"` from BoTorch's `scipy_minimize` / `L-BFGS-B` marginal-likelihood optimiser hitting status `ABNORMAL` early in the loop — the same failure mode 47.6b.3.2a's Done note documented. Once the BO loop aborts, the final HF re-eval is the only `_recommend_incumbent` call that actually runs through the strategy code path; the inner-loop variance-guard recommendation (which IS gated by the strategy per 47.6b.3.2c.2's "in-loop variance-guard's `_recommend_incumbent` call also threads `sentinel_x`" deviation) only fires if at least one acquisition iteration completes the GP fit, which it does not here for these seeds.
    2. **`_recommend_incumbent` was bypassed (4/5 seeds) or fired without a binding mask (1/5 seeds).** Per 47.6b.3.2c.4b.0's correction (the original wording at this position attributed inertness to 47.6b.3.1's clamp interacting with `eval_history`, which is wrong — the clamp at `bo.py:2049-2095` only writes to a local `kept_values` array that becomes `Y_train`; `eval_history` is never mutated, and `_collect_sentinel_x` at `bo.py:1175-1194` reads `e.value` directly so it correctly recovers all sentinel rows). The actual mechanism: **(a)** for the 4/5 seeds with early `error` exit (seeds 0, 1, 2, 4), `final_model` is `None` and the final-recommendation block at `bo.py:2396-2412` bypasses `_recommend_incumbent` entirely (the fallback picks the best HF observation directly), so neither voronoi nor any other strategy ever runs; **(b)** for seed 3 (39 HF evals, `final_model` non-None at the final step), `_recommend_incumbent` was called with `sentinel_x_final = _collect_sentinel_x(eval_history)` populated normally, but the voronoi mask either had no sentinel rows to filter against in the recommended region OR produced an argmin matching the unmasked argmin. The harness does not surface `extras.n_sentinel_per_fidelity` so the (a)-vs-(b) subcase split per seed cannot be distinguished post-hoc from this run; the structural correction is independent of which subcase fires for which seed.

    **Routing implication for 47.6b.3.2c.4d:** the voronoi strategy at default radius=0.1 does NOT close the basin-proximity gap on the multi-modal regression scaffold. The pass count is 0/5, identical to mean baseline. 47.6b.3.2c.4c (UCB strategy) is the next measurement; 47.6b.3.2c.4d will route based on whichever of {voronoi, ucb} clears the bar (or neither, in which case 47.6b.3.2d opens for path-(c) threshold revision per the recommended escalation order a → b → c).

    **Note for 47.6b.3.2c.4d / 47.6b.3.2c.4 (the parent tracker):** if the UCB strategy (47.6b.3.2c.4c) also misses, the dominant failure mode informing the routing decision is the early `error` exit on 4 of 5 seeds (0, 1, 2, 4): with `final_model is None` the final-recommendation block at `bo.py:2396-2412` bypasses `_recommend_incumbent` entirely, so no recommendation strategy (voronoi, ucb, or future) can ever run — the cost-aware utility's strategy choice is moot. A more impactful fix would be a GP-fit retry / fallback when `scipy_minimize` returns `ABNORMAL`, but that is beyond 47.6b.3.2c's scope (which is a recommendation-strategy item, not a GP-fit-resilience item). The original "voronoi-vs-clamp interaction" observation that previously occupied this paragraph was rescinded by 47.6b.3.2c.4b.0 — the unfiltered pre-clamp sentinel `x` set is ALREADY threaded via `_collect_sentinel_x(eval_history)` because the clamp does not mutate `eval_history`. Path-(c) (threshold revision per 47.6b.3.2d) remains the natural last-resort escalation.

    **NOTE:** see 47.6b.3.2c.4b.0 — done. Reason #2 and observation (i) above were rewritten in place by that fix; the empirical pass count `0/5` and the per-seed table are unaffected. The "clamp eats `_BO_SENTINEL` from `eval_history`" reasoning that previously occupied this Done note is incorrect (the clamp only writes to a local `Y_train` array and `eval_history` is unmodified); future 47.6b.3.2c.4c / 47.6b.3.2c.4d work should use the corrected diagnosis (`final_model is None` bypass at `bo.py:2396-2412` for early-`error`-exit seeds) instead.

- [x] **47.6b.3.2c.4b.0** Plan-text fix (residual from 47.6b.3.2c.4b's Done note in commit 739c855): the diagnosis under reason #2 of the "Two structural reasons" list (line 1787) and observation (i) of the "Note for 47.6b.3.2c.4d" paragraph (line 1791) are factually incorrect. They claim that 47.6b.3.1's clamp mechanism replaces sentinel rows in `eval_history` with finite values, so `_collect_sentinel_x(eval_history)` returns no sentinel `x` and the voronoi mask falls through to mean. But the clamp at `bo.py:2049-2095` only writes to a *local* `kept_values` list that becomes `Y_train` for the GP fit; `eval_history` itself is never mutated, and each `BOEval`'s `value` attribute remains the original `_BO_SENTINEL` for infeasible evals. `_collect_sentinel_x` (`bo.py:1175-1194`) reads `e.value` directly from `eval_history` and correctly returns sentinel rows whenever they exist. The proposed "future fix would be to thread the *pre-clamp* sentinel `x` set into `_recommend_incumbent`" in observation (i) is therefore based on a false premise — the unfiltered pre-clamp sentinel `x` set is ALREADY threaded via `_collect_sentinel_x(eval_history)`. The actual reason the voronoi mask was inert on this sweep is two-fold: **(a) for seeds where the BO loop terminates with `stop_reason="error"` before any GP fit succeeds, `final_model` is `None` and the final-recommendation block at `bo.py:2396-2412` bypasses `_recommend_incumbent` entirely (the fallback picks the best HF observation directly), so neither voronoi nor UCB ever runs**; **(b) for seeds where `final_model` is non-None at the final step (e.g. seed 3 with 39 HF evals), `_recommend_incumbent` does run, but voronoi fires only when `_collect_sentinel_x(eval_history)` returns non-empty — i.e., when the loop accumulated at least one infeasible eval before the error.** The harness does not surface `extras.n_sentinel_per_fidelity` so the per-seed subcase split between (a) and (b) cannot be distinguished post-hoc from this run, but the structural correction does not depend on which subcase fires for which seed. **Plan-text-only fix** — no production code or tests to change here. Mirrors the 47.6b.0 / 47.6b.3.0 / 47.6b.3.1.1 / 47.6b.3.2.0 / 47.6b.3.2c.0 / 47.6b.3.2c.1.0 / 47.6b.3.2c.2.0 pattern. **Do this before starting 47.6b.3.2c.4c** so 4c's Done note does not propagate the same misdiagnosis (UCB has no `sentinel_x` dependency at all, so 4c's diagnosis will naturally differ; but the broader habit of attributing inertness to the clamp must not carry over, and the bypass-when-`final_model is None` issue applies equally to UCB).

The clamp does NOT explain the inertness — `eval_history` is never mutated by the clamp.
